GIVEN THAT, IT'S ALL TOGETHER APPROPRIATE FOR COUNCIL TO PROVIDE POLICY LEVEL DIRECTION THROUGH THE FINANCIAL CRISIS AND THAT'S WHAT THIS RESOLUTION DOES. IN FACT, IT'S NOT JUST A PROGRAM, IT'S COUNCIL'S FUNDAMENTAL RON SUAREZ JOB TO PROVIDE POLICY DIRECTIONS IN TIMES LIKE THIS. POLICY DIRECTION WOULD BE HELPFUL, BUT THAT THERE MUST BE FLEXIBILITY THIS RESOLUTION HAS BOTH. THE POLICY DIRECTION TAKES THE FORM OF GENERALLY ENDORSING THE RECOVERY PLAN PRESENTED BY MR. CRAWFORD AND AFFIRMING ITS NECESSITY AND PROVIDING GUIDING PRINCIPLES AND EXPECTATIONS INCLUDING FISCAL RESPONSIBILITY, CHAIRED SACRIFICE AND COUNCIL AND SENIOR LEADERSHIP TAKING THE LEAD IN THAT SACRIFICE. THE NECESSARY FLEXIBILITY IS PROVIDED IN TWO PAYS. FIRST IT'S EXPLICITLY COVERED IN A SECOND TO LAST RESOLVE CLAUSE AND BY REMOVING THE COUNTY MILLAGE PROCEEDS. AND REGARDING THAT PARTICULAR ITEM, CONTRARY TO THE PUBLIC IMPRESSION THAT'S BEEN CREATED THAT RESOLVE CLAUSE DOESN'T DEFUND ANYTHING OR ANY A MONEY AWAY FROM ANYONE. RATHER IT SAYS WE WILL TREAT THOSE DOLLARS EXACTLY THE SAME AS WE DO FOR ALL OTHER UNRESTRICTED TAX DOLLARS. IF IN A GIVEN YEAR, THERE'S A NEED FOR ADDITIONAL MENTAL HEALTH SERVICES, OR FOR MORE AFOR THIBLE HOUSING, OR A NEED TO AVOID LAYING OFF EMPLOYEES, THE CITY NEEDS THE FLEXIBILITY TO DO THAT. I WOULD LIKE TO WATCH THROU THE RATIONAL FOR THE SPECIFIC ITEMS. I'M OPEN TO SUGGESTIONS AND AMENDMENTS. I HOPE THAT WE WILL ALL AGREE THAT IN THIS SITUATION WHEN COUNCIL IS APPROVING A BUDGET, ARGUABLY ONE OF THE MOST IMPORTANT THINGS WE DO AND WHEN WE ARE ABOUT TO NAVIGATE ONE OF THE MOST SIGNIFICANT FINANCIAL CRISIS THE CITY HAS FACED, THAT POLICY DIRECTION FROM COUNCIL IS BOTH APPROPRIATE AND NECESSARY.
